 subah uthakar tumhen phir kuch likhnaa he

 kyonki uske bina na to yahaan sujan singh park main subah hogi or na vahaan

 yani sab kuch sanskari dikhataa tha

 tum kabhi kisi aurat kaa, to kabhi kisi kitaab kaa zikr karte

 phir chep dete vah joke bhi

 kitna badmaash sardaar he ye

 magar tum likhte

 par tum bas itane hi nahin ho khushvanth

 safar lanbaa lagata tha tab

 kuch chuudi kaarobaari savaar the

 maine nowell maang liya

 neeche tumhaari chashme ke peeche se chhipi ankhen or laal pagadi najar ai

 kaan laal hone lage

 ye ek aadmi kii kahani thi, jo akhbaar main ishtehaar de auraton ko saath rahane bulaata tha

 padhin, magar jaise-jaise padhin, tumhaare bare main raay badalati gai

 dilli ke naam se

 uske baad padhe tumhaare patrakarita ke dinon ke kisse

 jab tumhaare pita sar shobhaa singh dilli bana rahe the

 tum mumbai gaye

 magar uske pehle ek veshya ke yahaan gaye

 tum har bitate din ke saath bebaak sachche hote rahe

 mumbai or dilli kii patrakarita bataai

 ho saktaa he tum rahe ho

 punjab kii samasya par mark tali kii kitaab ke saath-saath main tumhaari kitaab bhi jarur rickmond karata hum

 kya majaa diya sardaar tumne

 ki tumne quran padhaa he

 moonchhen anthne vaale us badmaash pakistani ko tumne chakit kiya or ham byaaj main chakit ho gaye

wrote apni shradhanjali bhi likhi or uske baad barason jie bhi

 muslim bujurg ko naukaraani se maje karvaa hi die

 par nahin
 i am wrong again
 maje ke paimaane par to tumhen zyaadaatar hindustan ne mapa he
 a chieftain who is frustrated
 jo sex, auraten or sharaab ke bare main likhata he or phir bhi mashhoor hua jaataa he

 ye khushvanth singh nahin he

 tum subah kitaaben pard rahe the

 or jab indira gandhi kii hatya ke baad har sardaar apni deshbhakti kaa ishtehaar maathe par taangane ko majaboor tha, tum tab bhi badgumaan state kii aisi taisi karne main lage the

 or phir bheetar ekant kii gyaan sadhana main lag gaye

 par ham to bhatke hue the baahar ke khushvanth main

 jo tumhaari mureed thim

 ham galat the khushvanth

 usamen funs tamaam log roshni khoj hi lenge

 yah agsit pole shuruaati chaar charnon ke matdaan ke aadhaar par kiya gaya he

 7 Anant Gupta, chief executive officer (CEO) of IT services company HCL Technologies, has resigned
 unke istife ke baad company ne mukhya parichaalan adhikari si vijayakumar ko padonnat kar siio niyukt kiya gaya he
 The company said in a statement, 'anant Gupta has decided to leave the company due to personal reasons
 ' bayaan ke anusaar company si vijay kumaar ko padonnat kar tatkaal prabhaav se adhyaksh or siio niyukt kar rahi he
 The comments echsiel technolajeej ke chairman or mukhya ranneeti adhikari shiv nadar ne kaha, '
 
 
 Vijay has always led the company from the front
 hamaari yatra ko aage badhaane main unka drushtikon or kaaryon kaa achche tareeke se nishpaadan kaa ricard behtareen he
 
 ' (hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) company ne ek bayaan main kaha, 'anant gupta ne vyaktigat kaarnon se company chhodane kaa faisla kiya he
 According to the statement, the company is promoting c Vijay Kumar and appointing the chairman and CEO with immediate effect
 tippaniyan HCL Technologies Chairman and Chief Strategy Officer Shiv Nadar said, '
 
 
 vijay ne hameshaa aage se company kaa netritv kiya he
 His vision and record of good execution of tasks is excellent in taking our journey forward

 (apart from the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, it has been published directly from the Syndicate feed
 )(hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) chhattisgarh ke raigarh jile kii ek adaalat ne naaballig bete kii hatya ke maamle main ek vyakti ko umrakaid kii sajaa sunai he
 It was a case of 'male sacrifice'
 sarkari vakil anil shrivastav ne bataaya ki vishesh adaalat ke nyaayadhish manish kumaar naidu ne ranvijay bharti ko kal umrakaid kii sajaa sunai
 The court also imposed a fine of Rs 5,000 on Bharti, a resident of Bhagwanpur village
 tippaniyan Srivastava said that Bharti had beheaded his 14-year-old son Chandan while offering 'male sacrifice' for the 'good' of his family
 (is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he
 It is published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) Government lawyer Anil Srivastava said that special court judge Manish Kumar Naidu sentenced Ranvijay Bharti to life imprisonment yesterday
 adaalat ne bhagavanpur gaanv ke nivasee bharti par 5,000 rupee kaa jurmaana bhi lagaaya

 ) (this news has not been edited by the NDTV team
 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) hindu jan-jagriti samiti (echgees) naam ke ek sanghathan ne aagaamee ganesh chaturthi se pehle plaster of paris se baniin ganesh kii murtiyon par pratibandh lagane kii maang kii he
 He says that these idols are against Hindu tradition and cause pollution
 sanghathan ne ise lekar goa kii paryaavaran mantri elina saldanha ko ek gyaapan bhi saunpa he
 HJS said in a statement, 'according to the science of spirituality, the sculptures should be made of shadu (clay)
 aajkal murti ke nirmaan main plaster of paris kaa istemaal kiya ja rahaa he kyonki yah halkaa or zyada aakarshak he
 The memorandum states that there is a reference in the Puranas that Ganapati was constructed from clay, therefore it is appropriate to use a clay idol made of clay made for worshiping
 bayaan main daawa kiya gaya ki ganpati ke pavitrak (shuddh aadhyatmik kan) chikani mitti kii bani murti kii taraf aakarshith hote hai
 The paper pulp statues are also opposed to the organization, the paper pulp figurines have also opposed, because their chemical based dyes cause water pollution
